可以简单地帮助用户快速激活Windows，而这种激活方式，永久有效。当重装系统以后，激活信息依然生效。</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Digital license is a simpler and more efficient way of activation/authorization newly adopted by Windows 10, which only relies on the configuration information of your computer hardware. After activating system for the first time, as long as you don’t change the CPU and other devices connected to the mainboard, you can feel free to connect to Microsoft server to repeatedly, automatically and permanently activate your Windows 10 at any moment, without having to input the product key again and again every time you install the system.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>For Windows 10, no matter how it is activated (upgrades from Windows 7/8.1, is a bought retail version, or is bound with BIOS, namely the MSDM license), the activation will be converted to a unique Digital License of the corresponding&#160;<a href=\"https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows-hardware/drivers/install/hardware-ids\">Hardware ID</a>&#160;(HWID). This license will be sent to and stored on Microsoft server, then each time you make a fresh install of Windows and connect to MS server successfully, it will activate this machine automatically. This license will remain in valid, until the hardware changes. Of course, binding it to your Microsoft account can achieve the goal of transferring your license to another machine with different hardware configuration.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>数字许可证是Windows 10新采用的更简单，更有效的激活/授权方式，仅依赖于计算机硬件的配置信息。首次激活系统后，只要您不更改CPU和连接到主板的其他设备，您就可以随时连接到Microsoft服务器，以反复，自动和永久激活您的Windows 10，而无需每次安装系统时都必须反复输入产品密钥。</p>\n\n\n\n<p>对于Windows 10，无论它是如何激活的（从Windows 7 / class=\"expandable\"> \n  <li></li> \n  <li></li> \n  <li> <h4>Classes</h4> </li> \n </ul> \n</div> \n<div id=\"content\"> \n <h1>Introduction</h1> \n <p>This guide describes Vidyo’s client library, which allows developers to add real-time communication capabilities to their applications using a simple API that spans multiple platforms (Windows, Mac, Linux, iOS, Android) and languages (C, Objective-C, C#, Java, Javascript).</p> \n <h1>Legal Notice</h1> \n <p>(c) 2006-2018 Vidyo Inc.,<br /> 433 Hackensack Avenue,<br /> Hackensack, NJ 07601.</p> \n <p>All rights reserved.</p> \n <p>The information contained herein is proprietary to Vidyo, Inc. and shall not be reproduced, copied (in whole or in part), adapted, modified, disseminated, transmitted, transcribed, stored in a retrieval system, or translated into any language in any form by any means without the express written consent of Vidyo, Inc.</p> \n <h1 id=\"VidyoConnector\">VidyoConnector</h1> \n <p>The videoconferencing API that handles all aspects of the media (audio/video) connection.</p> \n <h2>Constructor</h2> \n <h3>Syntax</h3> \n <pre class=\" language-javascript\"><code class=\" language-javascript\">VidyoConnector<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> <span class=\"token function\">VidyoConnectorConstruct</span><span class=\"token punctuation\">(</span>VidyoConnector<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> c<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token keyword\">const</span> LmiViewId<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> viewId<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> VidyoConnectorViewStyle viewStyle<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> LmiUint remoteParticipants<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token keyword\">const</span> char<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> logFileFilter<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token keyword\">const</span> char<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> logFileName<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token keyword\">const</span> LmiVoidPtr userData<span class=\"token punctuation\">)</span></code></pre> \n <h3>Parameters</h3> \n <table> \n  <tbody> \n   <tr> \n    <th>Name</th> \n    <th>Type</th> \n    <th>Description</th> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>c</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#VidyoConnector\">VidyoConnector*</a></td> \n    <td>The VidyoConnector object.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>viewId</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#LmiViewId\">const LmiViewId*</a></td> \n    <td>A platform-specific view ID where the VidyoConnector’s rendering window will be added as a child window. It will be used to render the preview and composite remote participants. When running custom layout on macOS, the core animation layer should be disabled on this view.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>viewStyle</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#VidyoConnectorViewStyle\">VidyoConnectorViewStyle</a></td> \n    <td>Type of the composite renderer which represents the visual style and behaviour.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>remoteParticipants</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#LmiUint\">LmiUint</a></td> \n    <td>Number of remote participants to composite into the window. Setting the value to 0 (zero) will render the preview only.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>logFileFilter</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#char\">const char*</a></td> \n    <td>A space-separated (or comma-separated) sequence of names of log levels, each optionally followed by a category. Categories are separated from levels by the character ‘@’. <p>Either a level or category may be specified as ‘all’ or ‘*’ (interchangeably), meaning all levels or categories. A level specified without a category is equivalent to a level@*.</p> <p>The levels are: ‘fatal’, ‘error’, ‘warning’, ‘info’, ‘debug’, ‘sent’, ‘received’, ‘enter’, and ‘leave’.</p> <p>The level may be prefixed by ‘-‘ or ‘!’ (interchangeably), meaning to remove the given level (or levels, see below) from the given category. The string ‘none’ is equivalent to ‘-all’.</p> <p>The first level in the list may be prefixed by ‘+’. If the first level begins with a ‘+’ or ‘-‘/’!’, the string is used to modify the listener’s existing levels and categories. Otherwise, unless the <code>add</code> parameter is true, the levels and categories specified in the string replace all existing levels and categories for the listener. The leading character ‘+’ may be present before other levels, but is ignored.</p> <p>Unless they are preceded by ‘=’, level names imply other levels as well. In particular, each of the levels ‘fatal’, ‘error’, ‘warning’, ‘info’, and ‘debug’ implies the levels higher than it, when specified positively; ‘sent’ and ‘received’ always imply each other; and ‘enter’ and ‘leave’ always imply each other.</p> <p>See VidyoConnectorGetLogCategories for determining the names and descriptions of registered categories.</p> <p>Level names are case-insensitive; category names are case-sensitive.</p> <p>Example: ‘all’ – all levels, all categories.</p> <p>Example: ‘all -enter’ – all categories, all levels but enter and leave.</p> <p>Example: ‘*@VidyoClient’ – all levels for the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘-*@VidyoClient’ – remove all levels from the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘debug’ – all categories, fatal, error, warning, info, and debug levels.</p> <p>Example: ‘=debug’ – all categories, debug level only.</p> <p>Example: ‘all -=enter’ – all categories, all levels but enter (leave is still included).</p> <p>Example: ‘error@VidyoClient’ – fatal and error only for the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘warning debug@VidyoClient’ – fatal, error, and warning for all categories; additionally, info and debug for the VidyoClient category.</p></td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>logFileName</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#char\">const char*</a></td> \n    <td>Full path to the file where the log should be stored; otherwise, NULL or empty string, in order to use the default OS-dependent writable path.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>userData</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#LmiVoidPtr\">const LmiVoidPtr</a></td> \n    <td>Arbitrary user data that can be retrieved later.</td> \n   </tr> \n  </tbody> \n </table> \n <h3>Returns</h3> \n <table> \n  <tbody> \n   <tr> \n    <th>Type</th> \n    <th>Description</th> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#VidyoConnector\">VidyoConnector*</a></td> \n    <td>The constructed object on success. NULL on failure.</td> \n   </tr> \n  </tbody> \n </table> \n <h1 id=\"VidyoConnectorEnumerations\" class=\"enumerations\">Enumerations</h1> \n <h2 about log events.</p> \n <h3>Syntax</h3> \n <pre class=\" language-javascript\"><code class=\" language-javascript\">LmiBool <span class=\"token function\">VidyoConnectorRegisterLogEventListener</span><span class=\"token punctuation\">(</span>VidyoConnector<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> c<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> VidyoConnectorOnLog onLog<span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token keyword\">const</span> char<span class=\"token operator\">*</span> filter<span class=\"token punctuation\">)</span></code></pre> \n <h3>Parameters</h3> \n <table> \n  <tbody> \n   <tr> \n    <th>Name</th> \n    <th>Type</th> \n    <th>Description</th> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>c</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#VidyoConnector\">VidyoConnector*</a></td> \n    <td>The VidyoConnector object.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>onLog</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#VidyoConnectorOnLog\">VidyoConnectorOnLog</a></td> \n    <td>Callback that is triggered for every new log record.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>filter</td> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#char\">const char*</a></td> \n    <td>A space-separated (or comma-separated) sequence of names of log levels, each optionally followed by a category. Categories are separated from levels by the character ‘@’. <p>Either a level or category may be specified as ‘all’ or ‘*’ (interchangeably), meaning all levels or categories. A level specified without a category is equivalent to a level@*.</p> <p>The levels are: ‘fatal’, ‘error’, ‘warning’, ‘info’, ‘debug’, ‘sent’, ‘received’, ‘enter’, and ‘leave’.</p> <p>The level may be prefixed by ‘-‘ or ‘!’ (interchangeably), meaning to remove the given level (or levels, see below) from the given category. The string ‘none’ is equivalent to ‘-all’.</p> <p>The first level in the list may be prefixed by ‘+’. If the first level begins with a ‘+’ or ‘-‘/’!’, the string is used to modify the listener’s existing levels and 45categories. Otherwise, unless the <code>add</code> parameter is true, the levels and categories specified in the string replace all existing levels and categories for the listener. The leading character ‘+’ may be present before other levels, but is ignored.</p> <p>Unless they are preceded by ‘=’, level names imply other levels as well. In particular, each of the levels ‘fatal’, ‘error’, ‘warning’, ‘info’, and ‘debug’ implies the levels higher than it, when specified positively; ‘sent’ and ‘received’ always imply each other; and ‘enter’ and ‘leave’ always imply each other.</p> <p>See VidyoConnectorGetLogCategories for determining the names and descriptions of registered categories.</p> <p>Level names are case-insensitive; category names are case-sensitive.</p> <p>Example: ‘all’ – all levels, all categories.</p> <p>Example: ‘all -enter’ – all categories, all levels but enter and leave.</p> <p>Example: ‘*@VidyoClient’ – all levels for the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘-*@VidyoClient’ – remove all levels from the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘debug’ – all categories, fatal, error, warning, info, and debug levels.</p> <p>Example: ‘=debug’ – all categories, debug level only.</p> <p>Example: ‘all -=enter’ – all categories, all levels but enter (leave is still included).</p> <p>Example: ‘error@VidyoClient’ – fatal and error only for the VidyoClient category.</p> <p>Example: ‘warning debug@VidyoClient’ – fatal, error, and warning for all categories; additionally, info and debug for the VidyoClient category.</p></td> \n   </tr> \n  </tbody> \n </table> \n <h3>Returns</h3> \n <table> \n  <tbody> \n   <tr> \n    <th>Type</th> \n    <th>Description</th> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td><a href=\"http://www.byshang.cn/?p=11233#LmiBool\">LmiBool</a></td> \n    <td>LMI_TRUE on success, LMI_FALSE on failure.</td> \n   </tr> \n  </tbody> \n </table> \n <h1 This indicates the degree of significance of the event.</p> \n <h3>Syntax</h3> \n <pre class=\" language-javascript\"><code class=\" language-javascript\">VidyoLogLevel</code></pre> \n <h3>Values</h3> \n <table> \n  <tbody> \n   <tr> \n    <th>Name</th> \n    <th>Description</th> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_FATAL</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes a fatal error. In all likelihood system execution will not be able to continue.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_ERROR</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes a continuable error. The system should be able to continue, but human intervention or diagnosis may be necessary.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_WARNING</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes a warning. Something has occurred which may require attention or action, but which is not actually erroneous.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_INFO</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes information which may be useful or informative to a user of the system. No problems are being reported.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_DEBUG</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes information which may be useful to a developer to understand the code. The information is not expected to be useful to users of the system.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_SENT</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes data that has been transmitted by the system.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_RECEIVED</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes data that has been received by the system.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_ENTER</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes the system entering a function.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_LEAVE</td> \n    <td>The event being logged describes the system leaving from a function.</td> \n   </tr> \n   <tr> \n    <td>VIDYO_LOGLEVEL_INVALID</td> \n    <td>A value that does not represent a valid log level. -1&#160;&#8220;password&#8221;&#160;得到一串MD5加密的字符串，如：&#160;$1$5NwpneO7$YD82DhVJxCQpQ4zahB1N01&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>3. 1代表编码的视频序列完全遵从A.2.1所有条款，0不一定。<br />\nconstraint_set1_flag1代表编码的视频序列完全遵从A.2.2所有条款，0不一定。<br />\nconstraint_set2_flag 1代表编码的视频序列完全遵从A.2.3所有条款，0不一定。<br />\n注意：当上面3位有任意一位设置为1时，意味着视频序列完全遵从A.2所有条款，当proifle_idc为44、100、110、122或244时，此三位必须为0。<br />\nconstraint_set3_flag (1)当profile_idc为66、77或88且level_idc为11时，1代表遵从Annex A for level 1b，0代表遵从Annex for level 1.1。<br />\n(2)当profile_idc为100或110，1代表遵从Annex A for the High 10 Intra profile，0不一定。<br />\n(3)当profile_idc为122，1代表遵从Annex A for the High 4:2:2 Intra profile，0不一定。<br />\n(4)当profile_idc为44，此数据位应设置为1,0是错误的。<br />\n(5)当profile_idc为244，1代表遵从Annex A for the High 4:4:4 Intra profile，0不一定。<br />\n(6)当profile_idc为66、77或88且level_idc不为11时，1保留给未来使用，应设置为0，同时解码器应该忽略此数据位的值。<br />\nconstraint_set4_flag (1)当profile_idc为77、88或100，1代表frame_mbs_only_flag等于1，0则表示frame_mbs_only_flag可能1可能0。<br />\n(2)当profile_idc为118或128,，1代表编码的视频序列遵从H.10.1.1的所有条款，0不一定。<br />\n(3)当profile_idc不为以上两条时，1保留给未来使用，应设置为0，同时解码器应该忽略此数据位的值。<br />\nconstraint_set5_flag (1)当profile_idc为77、88或100，1代表Bslice类型不存在于编码的视频序列中，0不一定。<br />\n(2)当profile_idc为118，1代表遵从H.10.1.2的所有条款，0不一定。<br />\n(3)当profile_idc不为以上两条时，1保留给未来使用，应设置为0，同时解码器应该忽略此数据位的值。<br />\nconstraint_set6_flag保留，设置为0。<br />\nconstraint_set7_flag保留，设置为0。</p>\n<h3>\nlevle_idc：</h3>\n<p>等级 最大比特率（BP、MP、EP）kbit/s
